This is a sample capture of I/O port operations when loading from disk,
including the boot process, a "dir" execution and running the "dump" command.

Note that input operations from port 8 (disk status register) are filtered 
out in this capture in order to show the read data more concisely (otherwise 
each data byte read from port 0A would be preceded by two reads from the
status register).
